# <a name="removed-or-deprecated-features-for-finance-and-operations"></a><span data-ttu-id="93130-103">Fjarlægðar eða úreltar aðgerðir fyrir Finance and Operations</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-103">Removed or deprecated features for Finance and Operations</span></span>

[!include [banner](../includes/banner.md)]

<span data-ttu-id="93130-104">Þetta efnisatriði lýsir eiginleikum sem hafa verið fjarlægðir eða úreltir fyrir Finance and Operations.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-104">This topic describes features that have been removed or deprecated for Finance and Operations.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93130-105">*Fjarlægður* eiginleiki er ekki lengur tiltækur í vörunni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-105">A *removed* feature is no longer available in the product.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="93130-106">*Úreltur* eiginleiki er ekki í virkri þróun og getur verið fjarlægður úr uppfærslum í framtíðinni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-106">A *deprecated* feature is not in active development and may be removed in a future update.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93130-107">Þessi listi er ætlað að hjálpa þér að íhuga þessar fjarlægingar og úreldingar fyrir eigin áætlanagerð.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-107">This list is intended to help you consider these removals and deprecations for your own planning.</span></span> 

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="93130-108">Frá og með útgáfu Finance and Operations í júlí 2017 með verkvangsuppfærslu 8, eru uppsetningargerðir merktar út frá sérhverjum eiginleika sem hefur verið fjarlægður eða úreltur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-108">Starting with the Finance and Operations July 2017 release with Platform update 8, the type of deployments are noted for each removed or deprecated feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-109">Allar fyrri útgáfur sem nefndar eru í þessu efnisatriði studdu aðeins dreifingar til skýjanna.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-109">All of the previous releases mentioned in this topic supported cloud deployments only.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93130-110">Ítarlegar upplýsingar um hluti í Finance and Operations má finna í [Tæknileg tilvísunarskjöl](https://mbs.microsoft.com/customersource/northamerica/AX/downloads/reports/axtechrefrep).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-110">Detailed information about objects in Finance and Operations can be found in the [Technical reference reports](https://mbs.microsoft.com/customersource/northamerica/AX/downloads/reports/axtechrefrep).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-111">Hægt er að bera saman mismunandi útgáfur þessara skýrslna til að fá upplýsingar um hluti sem hefur verið breytt eða hafa verið fjarlægðir í hverri útgáfu Finance and Operations.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-111">You can compare the different versions of these reports to learn about objects that have changed or been removed in each version of Finance and Operations.</span></span>

### <a name="data-management-staging-clean-up"></a><span data-ttu-id="93130-196">Hreinsun á sviðssetningu gagnastjórnunar</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-196">Data management staging clean up</span></span>
|   |  |

### <a name="deprecated-apis-and-future-breaking-changes"></a><span data-ttu-id="93130-364">Úrelt API og framtíðarskiptingar breytinga</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-364">Deprecated APIs and future breaking changes</span></span>

#### <a name="field-groups-containing-invalid-field-references"></a><span data-ttu-id="93130-365">Reitahópar sem innihalda ógilda tilvísanareiti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-365">Field groups containing invalid field references</span></span>

|   |  |
|------------|--------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="93130-366">**Ástæða úreldingar/fjarlægingar**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-366">**Reason for deprecation/removal**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93130-367">Mögulegt er fyrir skilgreiningar á lýsigögnum töflu að hafa reitahópa sem innihalda ógilda tilvísanareiti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-367">It is possible for table metadata definitions to have field groups containing invalid field references.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-368">Þetta vandamál er sem stendur flokkað sem *viðvörun þýðanda* frekar en *villa* sem þýðir að stofnun virkjanlegs pakka og uppsetning geti haldið áfram án þess að laga vandamálið.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-368">This issue is currently categorized as a *compiler warning* rather than an *error*, meaning that the deployable package creation and deployment can proceed without fixing the issue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-369">Ef sett upp getur það leitt til keyrsluvillu í Fjárhagsskýrslugerð og SQL Server Reporting Services (SSRS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-369">If deployed, this can cause runtime failures in Financial Reporting and SQL Server Reporting Services (SSRS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-370">Til að leysa þennan vanda þarf að:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-370">To fix this issue:</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="93130-371">1. Fjarlægja ógilda tilvísunarreitinn úr skilgreiningu töflureitahópsins.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-371">1. Remove the invalid field reference from the table field group definition.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="93130-372">2. Endurþýða.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-372">2. Recompile.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="93130-373">3. Tryggja að tekið sé á öllum viðvörunum og villum.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-373">3. Ensure any warnings or errors are addressed.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="93130-374">**Skipt út fyrir aðra eiginleika?**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-374">**Replaced by another feature?**</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="93130-375">Þessi viðvörun verður skipt út fyrir þýðingarvillu í framtíðinni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-375">This warning will be replaced by a compile error in the future.</span></span>  |

### <a name="extension-of-the-list-of-electronic-reporting-er-functions"></a><span data-ttu-id="93130-471">Útvíkkun listans yfir aðgerðir Rafrænnar skýrslugerðar</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-471">Extension of the list of Electronic reporting (ER) functions</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93130-472">Möguleikinn á að kynna sérsniðnar aðgerðir sem notaðar eru í ER-tjáningarbyggingu (til að fá frekari upplýsingar, sjá [Útvíkka lista yfir aðgerðir Rafrænnar skýrslugerðar (ER)](../../dev-itpro/analytics/general-electronic-reporting-formulas-list-extension.md)) er ekki studdur lengur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-472">The possibility to introduce custom functions to be used in the ER expression builder (for more information, see [Extend the list of Electronic reporting (ER) functions](../../dev-itpro/analytics/general-electronic-reporting-formulas-list-extension.md)) is not supported any more.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-473">Vegna breytinga á ER API, varð API til að kalla innbyggðar aðgerðir frá ER tjáningarbyggingu innra API og ekki hægt að útvíkka lengur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-473">Due to changes of the ER APIs, the API to call built-in functions from the ER expression builder became internal and can’t be extended any longer.</span></span>

|   |  |
|------------|--------------------|

| <span data-ttu-id="93130-476">**Skipt út fyrir aðra eiginleika?**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-476">**Replaced by another feature?**</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="93130-477">Ekkert.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-477">None.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-478">Í hvert skipti sem þörf er á nýrri innbyggðu aðgerð verður að senda nýtt framlengingarbeiðni til ER rammahópsins.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-478">Whenever a new built-in function is needed, a new extension request must be addressed to the ER framework team.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="93130-479">Sem tímabundið verk um það leyti sem umbeðin aðgerð er í þróun hjá ER teyminu er hægt að forrita nauðsynlega rökfræði sem aðferð sérsniðins umsóknarflokks.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-479">As a temporary work around while the requested function is under development by the ER team, the required logic can be programmed as a method of a custom application class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-480">Þessa aðferð er hægt að nálgast í ER-tjáningu sem eiginleika viðbætts ER-gagnasafns af **Umsókn/Flokkur** gerðinni sem vísar til þessa sérsniðna umsóknarflokks.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-480">This method can be accessed in an ER expression as a property of the added ER data source of the **Application\Class** type that refers to that custom application class.</span></span>  |

### <a name="data-partitions"></a><span data-ttu-id="93130-1151">Deildaskiptingar gagna</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1151">Data partitions</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="93130-1153">**Ástæða úreldingar/fjarlægingar**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1153">**Reason for deprecation/removal**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93130-1154">Gögn deildaskiptingar voru kynnt í Dynamics AX 2012 R2 til að virkja einangrun gagna.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1154">Data partitions were introduced in Dynamics AX 2012 R2 to enable data isolation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-1155">Í almennum aðstæðum, er Fyrirtæki með dótturfyrirtæki og gögn úr eitt dótturfyrirtæki ætti ekki að vera sýnileg fyrir aðra dótturfyrirtæki, jafnvel þótt bæði dótturfyrirtækjum er stjórnað af sömu tæknideild.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1155">In a common scenario, a company has subsidiaries, and the data from one subsidiary should not be visible to another subsidiary, even though both subsidiaries are managed by the same IT department.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-1156">Hins vegar var þörf á aukalegar forskriftir og sameiginlegur kostnaður í forritinu til að stofna nýja deildaskiptingar og færa inn í þær gög, og afrita deildaskiptingar gagna.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1156">However, extra scripts and management overhead throughout the program were required in order to create new partitions and populate them with data, and to back up partition data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-1157">Í skýið, þar sem við höfum aðgang að verkvangur sem þjónusta (PaaS) gagnagrunnsþjónustu (Microsoft Azure SQL Gagnagrunnur), er mikið áhrifaríkara að nota í gagnagrunninn sem einangrunargeymi en að framkvæma einangrunina í forritinu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1157">In the cloud, where we have access to platform as a service (PaaS) database services (Microsoft Azure SQL Database), it's much more efficient to use a database as the isolation container than to do isolation in the program.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-1158">Óháð því hvort deildaskipting gagna er krafist fyrir dótturfyrirtæki, fyrir marga leigjendur, eða einfaldlega fyrir kvörðun, trúum við því að aðstæður megi meðhöndla betur með mörgum tilvikum af Finance and Operations.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1158">Regardless of whether data partitioning is required for subsidiaries, for multiple tenants, or just for scale, we believe that the scenarios can be handled better through multiple instances of Finance and Operations.</span></span> |

### <a name="database-and-file-share-storage-for-attachments"></a><span data-ttu-id="93130-1165">Gagnagrunnur og geymsla fyrir samnýttar skár fyrir viðhengi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1165">Database and file share storage for attachments</span></span>

### <a name="product-builder"></a><span data-ttu-id="93130-1388">Vörusamsetning</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1388">Product builder</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93130-1389">Vörusamsetning (Product builder) var notaður til að setja saman á lifandi hátt vörur úr sölupöntun, innkaupapöntun, framleiðslupöntun, sölutilboð, verktilboð eða vöruþörf.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1389">Product builder was used to dynamically configure items from a sales order, purchase order, production order, sales quotation, project quotation, or item requirement.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-1390">Samkvæmt vörulíkani sem var með líkanabreytum gat notandinn velja gildi til að uppfylla kröfur viðskiptavinar og sækja einkvæmt afurðarafbrigði sem höfðu Uppskrift og leið.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1390">Based on a product model that had modeling variables, the user could select values to meet the customer requirements and get a unique product variant that had a BOM and route.</span></span>

|------------|--------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="93130-1391">**Ástæða úreldingar/fjarlægingar**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1391">**Reason for deprecation/removal**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93130-1392">Product builder birti X ++ kóða til að endanotenda og er ekki studdur í þessari útgáfu af Dynamics AX.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1392">Product builder exposed X++ code to end users and isn't supported in the current version of Dynamics AX.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-1393">Það hefur verið fjarlægð til að koma í veg fyrir tvíteknar viðhaldsvinnu á kóðagrunnum sem skarast.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1393">It has been removed to avoid duplicate maintenance efforts on overlapping, sizeable codebases.</span></span>  |

### <a name="virtual-company-accounts"></a><span data-ttu-id="93130-1486">Sýndarreikningsskil</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1486">Virtual company accounts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93130-1487">Sýndarfyrirtækjaeiginleiki er ekki lengur studd í Dynamics AX.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1487">The virtual companies feature is no longer supported in Dynamics AX.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-1488">Eiginleikinn sýndarfyrirtæki gerði notendum mögulegt að setja upp töflur sem mátti deila með hóp fyrirtækja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1488">The virtual companies feature let users set up tables that could be shared by a set of companies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-1489">Fyrir lýsingu á aðgerðinni sjá [reikningsskil og sýndarreikningsskil](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/aa834382(v=ax.10).aspx).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1489">For a description of the feature, see [Company accounts and Virtual company accounts](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/aa834382(v=ax.10).aspx).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-1490">Eiginleikinn vinnur með því að flokka töflur í söfn sem tilheyra sýndarfyrirtæki, sem eru hópar af fyrirliggjandi "raunverulegum" fyrirtæki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1490">The feature works by grouping tables into collections that are assigned to virtual companies, which are groups of existing “real” companies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-1491">Fyrirspurnir eru stofnaðar svo að öll fyrirtæki í sýndarfyrirtækinu hafi aðgang að gögnum í töflum tengdra töflusafna.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1491">Queries are created so that all the companies in the virtual company can access the data in the tables of the associated table collections.</span></span>

|   |  | 
|------------|--------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="93130-1492">**Ástæða úreldingar/fjarlægingar**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1492">**Reason for deprecation/removal**</span></span> | <span before data is stored in the tables.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-1494">Að bæta sýndarfyrirtæki eftirá við yfir fyrirliggjandi framkvæmd er mjög erfitt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1494">Retrofitting virtual companies onto an existing implementation is very difficult.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="93130-1495">- Þar sem hefur verið svo mikið um stöðlun gagna í gildandi útgáfu af Dynamics AX, er orðið mjög erfitt að vita hvað skuli bæta við töflusöfn.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1495">- Because there has been so much data normalization in the current version of Dynamics AX, it has become difficult to know what to add to the table collections.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-1496">Til dæmis er erfitt að from tables that are in a virtual company must also added.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93130-1498">Vegna Stöðlun Tafla verða jafnvel einfalt aðalgögn sem er dreift yfir margar töflur að vera hluti af sýndarfyrirtækinu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1498">Because of table normalization, even simple master data that is spread across multiple tables must be part of that is made here will cause functional issues.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="93130-1500">- Þegar tafla er hluti af sýndarfyrirtæki, tapar það upplýsingar um uppruna gagnanna, og aðeins sýndarfyrirtæki er skráð.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93130-1500">- When a table is part of a virtual company, it loses information about the origin of the data, and only the
